For the expensive sweaters that come from clothing print shops, if the shop is an actual small business then they have to charge that much for individual orders if theyâ€™re going to make a profit. The only way for you to really get a deal is to buy bulk. Plus, a lot of small business print shops make the print screens by hand and spread the design by hand too (automatic machines cost a buttload). That kind of repetitive work is really tough on shoulders so their price (if theyâ€™re smart) will also help set them up for future medical bills when they inevitably destroy their shoulders. My aunt and uncle own a clothing print shop and they once broke down their finances to me while explaining their prices.

I've been making my own vanilla for years.  I buy my beans from Amazon, use mid-quality vodka and you have vanilla.  It does have to sit for several weeks in order to steep but it's so much more economical than buying vanilla extract and it lasts forever. Piece of advice for anyone tempted to buy the puff sunscreen. To get the actual protection listed, you need about half a teaspoon for your face and neck (this varies between 1/4 and 1/2 teaspoon dependant upon the dermatologist). The puff will not give you anywhere near this amount, so will not protect you from the sun and I imagine the puff absorbs a lot of the product too.
